<p align=""left""><strong>The Digital Age<br />
</strong>   Digital image capture, storage and manipulation is ushering in a new age in microscopy.   Digital microscope cameras provide you a broader range of functionality, flexibility and portability,    expanding your capabilities beyond the traditional optical laboratory microscope.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p align=""left"">The Mighty Scope is lightweight, handy, and&nbsp;amazingly easy to use!   Plug&nbsp;it&nbsp;into the USB port of your PC or laptop and you're ready to go!   All it takes is a&nbsp;simple press of the Microtouch shutter trigger to quickly and convenient capture your magnified image.   With its high resolution magnification (10X - 200x), simple operation, and compact&nbsp;size,   The Mighty Scope&nbsp;puts the world of microphotography at your fingertips.</p>
<p align=""left"">CML#-313-050</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p align=""center""><a href=""http://www.cmlsupply.com/mightyscope/gallery/index.htm""><img height=""100"" alt=""Click for Gallery"" src=""http://www.cmlsupply.com/mightyscope/gallery/thumbnails/01b_Currency.jpg"" /></a> <a href=""http://www.cmlsupply.com/mightyscope/gallery/index.htm""><img height=""100"" alt=""Click for Gallery"" src=""http://www.cmlsupply.com/mightyscope/gallery/thumbnails/02a_Coin.jpg"" /></a> <a href=""http://www.cmlsupply.com/mightyscope/gallery/index.htm""><img height=""100"" alt=""Click for Gallery"" src=""http://www.cmlsupply.com/mightyscope/gallery/thumbnails/04b_CircuitBoard.jpg"" /></a> <a href=""http://www.cmlsupply.com/mightyscope/gallery/index.htm""><img height=""100"" alt=""Click for Gallery"" src=""http://www.cmlsupply.com/mightyscope/gallery/thumbnails/05b_Ring.jpg"" /></a> <a href=""http://www.cmlsupply.com/mightyscope/gallery/index.htm""><img height=""100"" alt=""Click for Gallery"" src=""http://www.cmlsupply.com/mightyscope/gallery/thumbnails/07b_Onion.jpg"" /></a></p>

            <p align=""left"">Easy to use, 6-LED hand-held digital microscope with a USB interface.</p>
            <p align=""left"">Can be used for science and engineering work, dermatology, detailed repair, assembly and quality control<br />
            (i.e. electronics, mechanical, etc), hobbies &amp; collecting (coin, stamp, watch, jewelry, etc.), law enforcement<br />
            (counterfeit ID, crime lab, etc), entertainment and much more.</p>
            <p align=""left"">High resolution magnification at your fingertips. Detailed examination of any area you choose.</p>
            <p align=""left"">LED intensity can be adjusted using control wheel on body, and<br />
            an adjustable magnification from10X - 200X, all in one compact lens.</p>
            <p align=""left"">Microtouch Shutter trigger allows for convenient image capture when in hand held mode or mounted<br />
            on a stand.</p>
            <p align=""left"">Mighty Scope comes with software for easy capture of images or videos (measurement function included) and<br />
            adjustable stand. Optional boom type stand is also available.</p>

<p><strong>0.7 ounce canister</strong></p>
<p>Plato's TT-95 LEAD FREE Tip Tinner is a fast, efficient, and safe means of re-tinning tips. This thermally-stable compound is residue free and environmentally and ESD-safe.</p>
<p>A well tinned soldering tip improves operator performance and satisfaction. Plato's TT95 Tip-Tin provides improved cleaning and re-tinning of highly oxidized soldering iron tips safely and efficiently. Just wipe the oxidized soldering tip at normal soldering temperature into the tip tinner for a few seconds until the bright tinning surrounds the working end of the tip, then wipe the excess residue on a wet cellulose sponge - it's that easy!</p>
